315 # plugin2 emulates a dynamic tracing plugin: the caller's locals

318 self.make_file("render.py", """\ 3.6.macos-latest.c3.6.ubuntu-latest.c3.6.windows-latest.c3.7.macos-latest.c3.7.ubuntu-latest.c3.7.windows-latest.c3.8.macos-latest.c3.8.ubuntu-latest.c3.8.windows-latest.c3.9.macos-latest.c3.9.ubuntu-latest.c3.9.windows-latest.c3.10.macos-latest.c3.10.ubuntu-latest.c3.10.windows-latest.c

320 # This function emulates a template renderer. The plugin 

321 # will examine the `filename` and `linenum` locals to

323 fiddle_around = 1 # not used, just chaff.

329 return x+1 

330 """)

484 import coverage.plugin 

485 class Plugin(coverage.CoveragePlugin): 

486 def file_tracer(self, filename): 

487 return OddTracer(filename) 

488 def file_reporter(self, filename): 

489 return "python" 

490 

491 class OddTracer(coverage.plugin.FileTracer): 

492 def __init__(self, filename): 

493 self.filename = filename 

494 def source_filename(self): 

495 return self.filename 

496 def line_number_range(self, frame): 

497 lineno = frame.f_lineno 

498 if lineno % 2: 

499 return (lineno, lineno) 

500 else: 

501 return (-1, -1) 

502 

503 def coverage_init(reg, options): 

504 reg.add_file_tracer(Plugin())

958 from coverage import CoveragePlugin 

959 

960 class Plugin(CoveragePlugin): 

961 def dynamic_context(self, frame): 

962 name = frame.f_code.co_name 

963 if name.startswith(("test_", "doctest_")): 

964 parts = name.split("_", 1) 

965 return "%s:%s" % (parts[0], parts[1].upper()) 

966 return None 

967 

968 def coverage_init(reg, options): 

969 reg.add_dynamic_context(Plugin()) 

970 """)
